Send electronic invoice, using legal format#

This endpoint is used to send eletronic invoice to your costumer/receiver using the portuguese CIUS-PT legal format.

After using this endpoint, a electronic invoice will be sent to your costumer/receiver to be integrated in their system.

Endpoint steps#

  1. Get a token from your credentials by calling the endpoint Account/getToken

  2. Send your invoice calling the asynchronous endpoint CountryFormatAsyncRequest/processDocument; the legal invoice format (XML CIUS-PT) is sent in the payload

  3. Check the result of your request using the received request id at CountryFormatAsyncRequest/{RequestId}

  4. Once the request has finished successfully you get back a document id; check the invoice integration status on your customer at endpoint OutboundFinancialDocument/{DocumentId}

Response structure from server#

When a request is well formed and the authentication data is correct the system responds with a message envelope as follows:

{
	"CorrelationId": "<GUID>", /* for correlation purposes */
	"IsValid": true,           /* false in case of erros */
	"Errors": [],              /* if empty is a good signal */
	"Data": "<Service Response Data>"   /* the data retuned ex: token, invoice status .. dependent on the endpoint called */
}

Endpoint Server Base URL#

# SANDBOX - Test Environment
server_base_adress = "dcn-solution.saphety.com/Dcn.Sandbox.WebApi"

# Saphety Invoice Network - Production Environment
#server_base_adress = "dcn-solution.saphety.com/Dcn.Business.WebApi"

1. Get a token (Account/getToken)#

Get a token from your account credentials using endpoint api/Account/getToken
Check here how to obtain an authentication token.

2. Send invoice request (CountryFormatAsyncRequest/processDocument)#

This endpoint is asynchrounous. Thousands of requests can be requested at the same time. For each request you receive immediately a request id. Use it to query the request status.

2.1 Request structure#

In the url you need to supply three parameters:

intlVatCode#

  • Description: Tax identification of the supplier/issuer entity (aka as vatNumber).

  • Required: Yes

  • Type: string

  • Example: “PT518576302”

  • Notes: Only accepts valid vatNumbers and filled with the countryCode prefix.

documentType#

  • Description: Type of document that is sent.

  • Required: Yes

  • Type: string

  • Allowed values: “INVOICE”, “CREDIT_NOTE”, “DEBIT_NOTE”, “INVOICE_RECEIPT”, “SIMPLIFIED_INVOICE”

  • Example: “INVOICE”

country#

  • Description: Contry code of the contry legal format. It is a fixed value since we sending invoices compliant for legal format of Portuguese legislation.

  • Required: Yes

  • Example: “PT”

2.2 Request body#

At endpoint body you need to supply the CIUS-PT XML of the invoice.

CIUS-PT XML format#

  • Description: The body of this endpoint it’s the CIUS-PT XML format of the invoice.

  • Required: Yes

  • Type: string

2.3 Request example#

# SIN endpoint url form sending invoices requires issuer NIF and country and the document type
issuer_nif = "PT507957547"
document_type = "INVOICE"

service_url = "https://""{ServerBaseUrl}/api/CountryFormatAsyncRequest/processDocument/{IssuerNIF}/{DocumentType}/PT""".format(
    ServerBaseUrl=server_base_adress,
    IssuerNIF=issuer_nif,
    DocumentType=document_type
)
print (service_url)

# request boby must be a valid CIUS-PT
body_cius_pt = """<?xml version="1.0" encoding="utf-8"?>
<ubl:Invoice xmlns:cac="urn:oasis:names:specification:ubl:schema:xsd:CommonAggregateComponents-2" 
xmlns:cbc="urn:oasis:names:specification:ubl:schema:xsd:CommonBasicComponents-2" xmlns:ubl="urn:oasis:names:specification:ubl:schema:xsd:Invoice-2">
  <cbc:CustomizationID>urn:cen.eu:en16931:2017#compliant#urn:feap.gov.pt:CIUS-PT:2.0.0</cbc:CustomizationID>
  <cbc:ID>INVOICE-API-DOC-00001</cbc:ID>
  <cbc:IssueDate>2020-12-31</cbc:IssueDate>
  <cbc:DueDate>2019-01-28</cbc:DueDate>
  <cbc:InvoiceTypeCode>380</cbc:InvoiceTypeCode>
  <cbc:DocumentCurrencyCode>EUR</cbc:DocumentCurrencyCode>
  <cac:OrderReference>
    <cbc:ID>ORD-001</cbc:ID>
  </cac:OrderReference>
  <cac:AdditionalDocumentReference>
    <cbc:ID schemeID="AAA">INVOICE-API-DOC-00001</cbc:ID>
    <cbc:DocumentTypeCode>130</cbc:DocumentTypeCode>
    <cbc:DocumentDescription>INVOICE_REPRESENTATION</cbc:DocumentDescription>
    <cac:Attachment>

    <cbc:InvoicedQuantity unitCode="C62">10.00</cbc:InvoicedQuantity>
    <cbc:LineExtensionAmount currencyID="EUR">100.00</cbc:LineExtensionAmount>
    <cac:Item>
      <cbc:Name>Item 1</cbc:Name>
      <cac:ClassifiedTaxCategory>
        <cbc:ID>S</cbc:ID>
        <cbc:Percent>23.00</cbc:Percent>
        <cac:TaxScheme>
          <cbc:ID>VAT</cbc:ID>
        </cac:TaxScheme>
      </cac:ClassifiedTaxCategory>
    </cac:Item>
    <cac:Price>
      <cbc:PriceAmount currencyID="EUR">10.00</cbc:PriceAmount>
    </cac:Price>
  </cac:InvoiceLine>
</ubl:Invoice>
"""

https://dcn-solution.saphety.com/Dcn.Sandbox.WebApi/api/CountryFormatAsyncRequest/processDocument/PT507957547/INVOICE/PT

* Note: the payload example showed here is a sample created by Saphety, you can use another cius-pt payload with your data, as long as it is a valid one.

2.3 Call endpoint and get back the request id#

Send your electronic invoice using the endpoint /api/CountryFormatAsyncRequest/processDocument/:intlVatCode/:documentType/:country, then record the request id from response Data.

# build the request
headers = {
    'Content-Type': 'application/xml',
    'Authorization': 'bearer ' + token
    }
# POST request to send the invoice
response = requests.request("POST", service_url, data=body_cius_pt, headers=headers)

# formating the response to json for visualization purposes only
json_response = json.loads(response.text)
print(json.dumps(json_response, indent=4))

# your request id is at:
request_id = json_response["Data"];

{
    "CorrelationId": "f6ef8ee6-9e28-4612-bec4-7502e05415a0",
    "IsValid": true,
    "Errors": [],
    "Data": "c5a88c1a-219b-4218-a157-edd5c5e62b06"
}

3. Check the success of your request (CountryFormatAsyncRequest/{RequestId})#

Get the request status by the request id using the endpoint /api/CountryFormatAsyncRequest/:id

3.1 Build the endpoint url#

In the url you need to supply the request id received

https://<ServerBaseUrl>/CountryFormatAsyncRequest/<RequestId>

# SIN endpoint url for retrieving the status of a process

service_url = "https://" + server_base_adress + "/api/CountryFormatAsyncRequest/" + request_id
print (service_url)

https://dcn-solution.saphety.com/Dcn.Sandbox.WebApi/api/CountryFormatAsyncRequest/c5a88c1a-219b-4218-a157-edd5c5e62b06

3.2 Check your request status#

# build the request
headers = {
    'Authorization': 'bearer ' + token
    }
# POST request to send the invoice
response = requests.request("GET", service_url, headers=headers)
# formating the response to json for visualization purposes only
json_response = json.loads(response.text)

# Your status:
status = json_response["Data"]
outbound_financial_document_id = None
#print(json.dumps(json_response, indent=4))

#request status (Queued, Running, Error, Finished)
request_status = json_response["Data"]["AsyncStatus"]

if request_status == "Finished":
    print ("Your request has finished.")
    outbound_financial_document_id = json_response["Data"]["OutboundFinancialDocumentId"]
    print("You have created the outbound document id: " + outbound_financial_document_id)

Your request has finished.
You have created the outbound document id: c720b060-6849-40ee-a2cd-143c3e32486e


Your request status is at response.Data.AsyncStatus, see the possible values:

“Queued”: The request is in queue to be processed. Check the status again in a few seconds.

“Running”: The request is still runnig. Check the status again in a few seconds.

“Error”: Your request has finished with errors. Check the error list at response.Data.ErrorList. You need to correct the errors and submit the document again (new request).

“Finished”: Your request has finished without errors. The request has created the outbound document id at response.Data.OutboundFinancialDocumentId. With “OutboundFinancialDocumentId” you can query the system for invoice notification status using the endpoint /api/OutboundFinancialDocument/:id.

4. Check the invoice integration status (OutboundFinancialDocument/{DocumentId})#

Get the invoice integration status by the Document id (response “OutboundFinancialDocumentId“) using endpoint OutboundFinancialDocument/:id

4.1 Build the endpoint url#

In the url you need to supply the outbound financial document id received.

https://<ServerBaseUrl>/OutboundFinancialDocument/<OutboundFinancialDocumentId>

# SIN endpoint url for retrieving inforfation on invoice previously sent
service_url = "https://"+ server_base_adress +"/api/OutboundFinancialDocument/" + outbound_financial_document_id
print (service_url)

https://dcn-solution.saphety.com/Dcn.Sandbox.WebApi/api/OutboundFinancialDocument/c720b060-6849-40ee-a2cd-143c3e32486e

4.2 Get the invoice integration status#

# build the request
headers = {

    }

response = requests.request("GET", service_url, headers=headers)

# formating the response to json for visualization purposes only
json_response = json.loads(response.text)
print(json.dumps(json_response, indent=4))

    "IsValid": true,
    "Errors": [],
    "Data": {
        "Id": "c720b060-6849-40ee-a2cd-143c3e32486e",
        "VirtualOperatorCode": null,
        "CompanyIntlVatCode": "PT507641230",

        "DocumentNumber": "FTSCN 2020/00000346",
        "ReceiverIntlVatCode": "PT507957547",
        "ReceiverName": "SAPHETY LEVEL - TRUSTED SERVICES, S.A",

        "DocumentTotal": 11.07,

        "NotificationStatus": "Delivered",

        "LastUpdateDate": "2021-01-03 00:00:00",
        "AuthorId": "e199d2e6-c1e8-4f7c-bb1e-01ea815c31f3",
        "Errors": null,
        "CreationDate": "2021-01-01 00:00:00"
    }
}

The integration status of an electronic invoice in archive is returned at “Data.IntegrationStatus” parameter.
IntegrationStatus, indicates the current integration status that the electronic invoice has in archive, see the possible values returned:

  • NotIntegrated - electronic invoice not sent to receiver entity for integration

  • Not_Sent - electronic invoice not sent for receiver entity

  • Error - electronic invoice with errors, not sent to receiver entity for integration

  • Sent - electronic invoice sent to receiver entity for integration

  • Received - electronic invoice sent to receiver entity for integration, receiver entity has confirmed its reception

  • Rejected - electronic invoice sent to receiver entity for integration, receiver entity is rejecting it

  • Paid - electronic invoice sent to receiver entity for integration, receiver entity is confirming it as paid

[Important note_1] When an electronic invoice is sent to a receiver entity outside Saphety network, the integration status will always be “NotIntegrated”. In this scenario the electronic invoice may have also a notification status (Sent, Delivered, Read or Error) if the CIUS-PT XML has the tag BT-49 filled in with the receiver entity’s email address (ex: <cbc:EndpointID schemeID=”EM”>eee@hh.pt</cbc:EndpointID>), otherwise the document will have integration status as “NotIntegrated” and notification status as “NoEmails”.

[Important note_2] When an electronic invoice is sent to a receiver entity of a network with interoperability, but the issuer does not have an approved connection to this network, the integration status will always be “NotIntegrated”. In this scenario the electronic invoice may have also a notification status (Sent, Delivered, Read or Error) if the CIUS-PT XML has the tag BT-49 filled in with the receiver entity’s email address (ex: <cbc:EndpointID schemeID=”EM”>eee@hh.pt</cbc:EndpointID>), otherwise the document will have integration status as “NotIntegrated” and notification status as “NoEmails”.

Use the OutboundFinancialDocumentId for any future checks on the invoice.
